<div class="postcell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
                    
<p>I often have to sort a dictionary, consisting of keys &amp; values, by value. For example, I have a hash of words and respective frequencies, that I want to order by frequency.</p>

<p>There is a <code>SortedList</code> which is good for a single value (say frequency), that I want to map it back to the word.</p>

<p><a href="http://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/f7fta44c.aspx" rel="noreferrer">SortedDictionary</a> orders by key, not value. Some resort to a <a href="http://www.codeproject.com/KB/recipes/lookupcollection.aspx" rel="noreferrer">custom class</a>, but is there a cleaner way?</p>
    </div>

<a name="298"></a>
<div id="answer-298" class="answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="298"  itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="298">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="528">528</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/298/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Use:</p>

<pre><code>using System.Linq.Enumerable;
...
List&lt;KeyValuePair&lt;string, string&gt;&gt; myList = aDictionary.ToList();

myList.Sort(
    delegate(KeyValuePair&lt;string, string&gt; pair1,
    KeyValuePair&lt;string, string&gt; pair2)
    {
        return pair1.Value.CompareTo(pair2.Value);
    }
);
</code></pre>

<p>Since you're targeting .NET 2.0 or above, you can simplify this into lambda syntax -- it's equivalent, but shorter. If you're targeting .NET 2.0 you can only use this syntax if you're using the compiler from Visual&nbsp;Studio&nbsp;2008 (or above).</p>

<pre><code>var myList = aDictionary.ToList();

myList.Sort((pair1,pair2) =&gt; pair1.Value.CompareTo(pair2.Value));
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
            <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2008-08-02T01:15:42"></time>
            <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div id="answer-1332" class="answer" data-answerid="1332"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="1332">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="531">531</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/1332/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Use LINQ:</p>

<pre><code>Dictionary&lt;string, int&gt; myDict = new Dictionary&lt;string, int&gt;();
myDict.Add("one", 1);
myDict.Add("four", 4);
myDict.Add("two", 2);
myDict.Add("three", 3);

var sortedDict = from entry in myDict orderby entry.Value ascending select entry;
</code></pre>

<p>This would also allow for great flexibility in that you can select the top 10, 20 10%, etc. Or if you are using your word frequency index for <code>type-ahead</code>, you could also include <code>StartsWith</code> clause as well.</p>
    </div>

                <span class="comment-copy">I&#39;m not sure if it always works because iterating over dictionary doesn&#39;t guarantee  that KeyValuePairs are &quot;pulled&quot; in the same order they have been inserted. Ergo, it doesn&#39;t matter if you use orderby in LINQ because Dictionary can change order of inserted elements. It usually works as expected but there is NO GUARANTEE, especially for large dictionaries.</span>

                <span class="comment-copy">Please disregard all suggestions of <code>.ToDictionary</code> - <a href="http://stackoverflow.com/a/4007787/1860652">standard dictionaries do not guarantee a sort order</a></span>

                       title="6,864 reputation"

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<pre><code>var ordered = dict.OrderBy(x =&gt; x.Value).ToDictionary(x =&gt; x.Key, x =&gt; x.Value);
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div id="answer-291" class="answer" data-answerid="291"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="291">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="168">168</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/291/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Looking around, and using some C# 3.0 features we can do this:</p>

<pre><code>foreach (KeyValuePair&lt;string,int&gt; item in keywordCounts.OrderBy(key=&gt; key.Value))
{ 
    // do something with item.Key and item.Value
}
</code></pre>

<p>This is the cleanest way I've seen and is similar to the Ruby way of handling hashes.</p>
    </div>

<a name="6438343"></a>
<div id="answer-6438343" class="answer" data-answerid="6438343"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="6438343">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="161">161</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/6438343/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>You can sort a Dictionary by value and save it back to itself (so that when you foreach over it the values come out in order):</p>

<pre><code>dict = dict.OrderBy(x =&gt; x.Value).ToDictionary(x =&gt; x.Key, x =&gt; x.Value);
</code></pre>

<p>Sure, it may not be correct, but it works.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<a name="292"></a>
<div id="answer-292" class="answer" data-answerid="292"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="292">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="61">61</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/292/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>On a high level, you have no other choice than to walk through the whole Dictionary and look at each value.</p>

<p>Maybe this helps:
<a href="http://bytes.com/forum/thread563638.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">http://bytes.com/forum/thread563638.html</a>
Copy/Pasting from John Timney:</p>

<pre class="lang-cs prettyprint-override"><code>Dictionary&lt;string, string&gt; s = new Dictionary&lt;string, string&gt;();
s.Add("1", "a Item");
s.Add("2", "c Item");
s.Add("3", "b Item");

List&lt;KeyValuePair&lt;string, string&gt;&gt; myList = new List&lt;KeyValuePair&lt;string, string&gt;&gt;(s);
myList.Sort(
    delegate(KeyValuePair&lt;string, string&gt; firstPair,
    KeyValuePair&lt;string, string&gt; nextPair)
    {
        return firstPair.Value.CompareTo(nextPair.Value);
    }
);
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
            <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2008-08-02T00:47:48"></time>

<a name="382462"></a>
<div id="answer-382462" class="answer" data-answerid="382462"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="382462">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="25">25</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/382462/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>You'd never be able to sort a dictionary anyway.  They are not actually ordered.  The guarantees for a dictionary are that the key and value collections are iterable, and values can be retrieved by index or key, but there is no guarantee of any particular order.  Hence you would need to get the name value pair into a list.</p>
    </div>

<a name="13854099"></a>
<div id="answer-13854099" class="answer" data-answerid="13854099"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="13854099">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="21">21</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/13854099/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>You do not sort entries in the Dictionary. Dictionary class in .NET is implemented as a hashtable - this data structure is not sortable by definition.</p>

<p>If you need to be able to iterate over your collection (by key) - you need to use SortedDictionary, which is implemented as a Binary Search Tree.</p>

<p>In your case, however the source structure is irrelevant, because it is sorted by a different field. You would still need to sort it by frequency and put it in a new collection sorted by the relevant field (frequency). So in this collection the frequencies are keys and words are values. Since many words can have the same frequency (and you are going to use it as a key) you cannot use neither Dictionary nor SortedDictionary (they require unique keys). This leaves you with a SortedList.</p>

<p>I don't understand why you insist on maintaining a link to the original item in your main/first dictionary. </p>

<p>If the objects in your collection had a more complex structure (more fields) and you needed to be able to efficiently access/sort them using several different fields as keys - You would probably need a custom data structure that would consist of the main storage that supports O(1) insertion and removal (LinkedList) and several indexing structures - Dictionaries/SortedDictionaries/SortedLists. These indexes would use one of the fields from your complex class as a key and a pointer/reference to the LinkedListNode in the LinkedList as a value.</p>

<p>You would need to coordinate insertions and removals to keep your indexes in sync with the main collection (LinkedList) and removals would be pretty expensive I'd think.
This is similar to how database indexes work - they are fantastic for lookups but they become a burden when you need to perform many insetions and deletions.</p>

<p>All of the above is only justified if you are going to do some look-up heavy processing. If you only need to output them once sorted by frequency then you could just produce a list of (anonymous) tuples:</p>

<pre><code>var dict = new SortedDictionary&lt;string, int&gt;();
// ToDo: populate dict

var output = dict.OrderBy(e =&gt; e.Value).Select(e =&gt; new {frequency = e.Value, word = e.Key}).ToList();

foreach (var entry in output)
{
    Console.WriteLine("frequency:{0}, word: {1}",entry.frequency,entry.word);
}
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<div id="answer-31514791" class="answer" data-answerid="31514791"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="31514791">

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/31514791/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<pre><code>Dictionary&lt;string, string&gt; dic= new Dictionary&lt;string, string&gt;();
var ordered = dic.OrderBy(x =&gt; x.Value);
return ordered.ToDictionary(t =&gt; t.Key, t =&gt; t.Value);
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Or for fun you could use some LINQ extension goodness:</p>

<pre><code>var dictionary = new Dictionary&lt;string, int&gt; { { "c", 3 }, { "a", 1 }, { "b", 2 } };
dictionary.OrderBy(x =&gt; x.Value)
  .ForEach(x =&gt; Console.WriteLine("{0}={1}", x.Key,x.Value));
</code></pre>
    </div>

<a name="2697521"></a>
<div id="answer-2697521" class="answer" data-answerid="2697521"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="2697521">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="10">10</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/2697521/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Sorting a <code>SortedDictionary</code> list to bind into a <code>ListView</code> control using VB.NET:</p>

<pre><code>Dim MyDictionary As SortedDictionary(Of String, MyDictionaryEntry)

MyDictionaryListView.ItemsSource = MyDictionary.Values.OrderByDescending(Function(entry) entry.MyValue)

Public Class MyDictionaryEntry ' Need Property for GridViewColumn DisplayMemberBinding
    Public Property MyString As String
    Public Property MyValue As Integer
End Class
</code></pre>

<p>XAML:</p>

<pre><code>&lt;ListView Name="MyDictionaryListView"&gt;
    &lt;ListView.View&gt;
        &lt;GridView&gt;
            &lt;GridViewColumn DisplayMemberBinding="{Binding Path=MyString}" Header="MyStringColumnName"&gt;&lt;/GridViewColumn&gt;
            &lt;GridViewColumn DisplayMemberBinding="{Binding Path=MyValue}" Header="MyValueColumnName"&gt;&lt;/GridViewColumn&gt;
         &lt;/GridView&gt;
    &lt;/ListView.View&gt;
&lt;/ListView&gt;
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<a name="35645695"></a>
<div id="answer-35645695" class="answer" data-answerid="35645695"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35645695">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="7">7</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/35645695/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>The other answers are good, if all you want is to have a "temporary" list sorted by Value. However, if you want to have a dictionary sorted by <code>Key</code> that <em>automatically synchronizes</em> with another dictionary that is sorted by <code>Value</code>, you could use the <a href="http://ecsharp.net/doc/code/classLoyc_1_1Collections_1_1Bijection.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>Bijection&lt;K1, K2&gt;</code> class</a>.</p>

<p><code>Bijection&lt;K1, K2&gt;</code> allows you to initialize the collection with two existing dictionaries, so if you want one of them to be unsorted, and you want the other one to be sorted, you could create your bijection with code like</p>

<pre><code>var dict = new Bijection&lt;Key, Value&gt;(new Dictionary&lt;Key,Value&gt;(), 
                               new SortedDictionary&lt;Value,Key&gt;());
</code></pre>

<p>You can use <code>dict</code> like any normal dictionary (it implements <code>IDictionary&lt;K, V&gt;</code>), and then call <code>dict.Inverse</code> to get the "inverse" dictionary which is sorted by <code>Value</code>.</p>

<p><code>Bijection&lt;K1, K2&gt;</code> is part of <a href="http://core.loyc.net/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Loyc.Collections.dll</a>, but if you want, you could simply copy the <a href="https://github.com/qwertie/Loyc/blob/master/Core/Loyc.Collections/Other/Bijection.cs" rel="nofollow noreferrer">source code</a> into your own project.</p>

<p><strong>Note</strong>: In case there are multiple keys with the same value, you can't use <code>Bijection</code>, but you could manually synchronize between an ordinary <code>Dictionary&lt;Key,Value&gt;</code> and a <a href="http://loyc.net/doc/code/classLoyc_1_1Collections_1_1BMultiMap_3_01K_00_01V_01_4.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>BMultiMap&lt;Value,Key&gt;</code></a>.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

            <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<a name="2569558"></a>
<div id="answer-2569558" class="answer" data-answerid="2569558"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="2569558">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="7">7</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/2569558/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>The easiest way to get a sorted Dictionary is to use the built in <code>SortedDictionary</code> class:</p>
<pre><code>//Sorts sections according to the key value stored on &quot;sections&quot; unsorted dictionary, which is passed as a constructor argument
System.Collections.Generic.SortedDictionary&lt;int, string&gt; sortedSections = null;
if (sections != null)
{
    sortedSections = new SortedDictionary&lt;int, string&gt;(sections);
}
</code></pre>
<p><code>sortedSections</code> will contain the sorted version of <code>sections</code></p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">

                <span class="comment-copy">As you mention in your comment, <code>SortedDictionary</code> sorts by keys.  The OP wants to sort by value.  <code>SortedDictionary</code> doesn&#39;t help in this case.</span>

    <li id="comment-29078926" class="comment js-comment " data-comment-id="29078926">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
            <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">Well... If he/she (you) can, just set the values as the keys.  I timed the operations and <code>sorteddictionary()</code> always won out by at least 1 microsecond, and it&#39;s much easier to manage (as the overhead of converting it back into something easily interacted with and managed similarly to a Dictionary is 0 (it is already a <code>sorteddictionary</code>)).</span>

<a name="54885808"></a>
<div id="answer-54885808" class="answer" data-answerid="54885808"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="54885808">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="4">4</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/54885808/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Actually in C#, dictionaries don't have sort() methods.
As you are more interested in sort by values,
you can't get values until you provide them key.
In short, you need to iterate through them using LINQ's <code>OrderBy()</code>,</p>
<pre><code>var items = new Dictionary&lt;string, int&gt;();
items.Add(&quot;cat&quot;, 0);
items.Add(&quot;dog&quot;, 20);
items.Add(&quot;bear&quot;, 100);
items.Add(&quot;lion&quot;, 50);

// Call OrderBy() method here on each item and provide them the IDs.
foreach (var item in items.OrderBy(k =&gt; k.Key))
{
    Console.WriteLine(item);// items are in sorted order
}
</code></pre>
<p>You can do one trick:</p>
<pre><code>var sortedDictByOrder = items.OrderBy(v =&gt; v.Value);
</code></pre>
<p>or:</p>
<pre><code>var sortedKeys = from pair in dictName
            orderby pair.Value ascending
            select pair;
</code></pre>
<p>It also depends on what kind of values you are storing: single (like string, int) or multiple (like List, Array, user defined class).
If it's single you can make list of it and then apply sort.<br />
If it's user defined class, then that class must implement IComparable, <code>ClassName: IComparable&lt;ClassName&gt;</code> and override <code>compareTo(ClassName c)</code> as they are more faster and more object oriented than LINQ.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="28275964">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/28275964/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Suppose we have a dictionary as </p>

<pre><code>   Dictionary&lt;int, int&gt; dict = new Dictionary&lt;int, int&gt;();
   dict.Add(21,1041);
   dict.Add(213, 1021);
   dict.Add(45, 1081);
   dict.Add(54, 1091);
   dict.Add(3425, 1061);
   sict.Add(768, 1011);
</code></pre>

<p>1) you can use <strong><code>temporary dictionary to store values as</code></strong> :</p>

<pre><code>        Dictionary&lt;int, int&gt; dctTemp = new Dictionary&lt;int, int&gt;();

        foreach (KeyValuePair&lt;int, int&gt; pair in dict.OrderBy(key =&gt; key.Value))
        {
            dctTemp .Add(pair.Key, pair.Value);
        }
</code></pre>
    </div>

<a name="61875551"></a>
<div id="answer-61875551" class="answer" data-answerid="61875551"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="61875551">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/61875551/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Required namespace : <code>using System.Linq;</code></p>

<pre><code>Dictionary&lt;string, int&gt; counts = new Dictionary&lt;string, int&gt;();
counts.Add("one", 1);
counts.Add("four", 4);
counts.Add("two", 2);
counts.Add("three", 3);
</code></pre>

<p>Order by desc :</p>

<pre><code>foreach (KeyValuePair&lt;string, int&gt; kvp in counts.OrderByDescending(key =&gt; key.Value))
{
// some processing logic for each item if you want.
}
</code></pre>

<p>Order by Asc :</p>

<pre><code>foreach (KeyValuePair&lt;string, int&gt; kvp in counts.OrderBy(key =&gt; key.Value))
{
// some processing logic for each item if you want.
}
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="grid fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
            <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2020-05-18T17:35:06"></time>

<div id="answer-11630804" class="answer" data-answerid="11630804"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="11630804">

                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/11630804/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>You can sort the Dictionary by value and get the result in dictionary using the code below:</p>

<pre><code>Dictionary &lt;&lt;string, string&gt;&gt; ShareUserNewCopy = 
       ShareUserCopy.OrderBy(x =&gt; x.Value).ToDictionary(pair =&gt; pair.Key,
                                                        pair =&gt; pair.Value);                                          
</code></pre>
    </div>

<a name="23975034"></a>
<div id="answer-23975034" class="answer" data-answerid="23975034"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="23975034">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="-2">-2</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/23975034/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Given you have a dictionary you can sort them directly on values using below one liner:</p>

<pre><code>var x = (from c in dict orderby c.Value.Order ascending select c).ToDictionary(c =&gt; c.Key, c=&gt;c.Value);
</code></pre>
    </div>
